# MaisonoryHome (https://maisonoryhome.com)

> MaisonoryHome is a modern home & living online store offering curated kitchen essentials, tabletop decor, candles, and minimalist home accessories. We focus on functional, stylish products designed for contemporary homes, serving customers primarily in the United States.
